- Generating offline data for 18,000 examples (6000 posCou + 6000 posAnc + 6000 negCouAnc), with K=4, takes 47.83 mins to be exact.

- Generating offline data for 18,000 examples (6000 posCou + 6000 posAnc + 6000 negCouAnc), with K=2, takes 34.15 mins to be exact.
- Generating offline data for 18,000 examples (6000 posCou + 6000 posAnc + 6000 negCouAnc), with K=1, takes 32.73 mins to be exact.
- Generating offline data for 18,000 examples (6000 posCou + 6000 posAnc + 6000 negCouAnc), with K=0, takes 31.65 mins to be exact.

This is on gargamel.cs.uiuc.edu: using PMI

** CIKM 09

*** Command Lines

- Generating GOLD corpus: 4 types
java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/cikm09/data/www07-classes.txt 5000 0 ../data/cikm09/data/5000_Neg.gold
java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/cikm09/data/www07-classes.txt 5000 1 ../data/cikm09/data/5000_Pos_Class_Entity.gold
java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/cikm09/data/www07-classes.txt 5000 2 ../data/cikm09/data/5000_Pos_Entity_Class.gold
java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/cikm09/data/www07-classes.txt 5000 3 ../data/cikm09/data/5000_Pos_Entity_Entity.gold

- Concatenate all GOLD corpora
cat 5000_Neg.gold 5000_Pos_Class_Entity.gold 5000_Pos_Entity_Class.gold 5000_Pos_Entity_Entity.gold > 5000_All.gold

- Permuting the whole corpus
java -jar Jupiter.jar PermuteData ../data/cikm09/data/5000_All.gold ../data/cikm09/data/5000_All_Permute.gold

- Feature extraction
java -jar Jupiter.jar ExtractFeatures /scratch/quangdo2/pages_xml_indexed_jupiter_category /scratch/quangdo2/pages_xml_indexed_jupiter_category.map /scratch/quangdo2/bigramTitleMapping.txt ../data/cikm09/data/5000_All_Permute.gold ../data/cikm09/data/5000_All_Permute.inter
This take 5096.411 seconds (20,000 examples) on gargamel, with K = 3.

------------

From the beginning.

- Generate GOLD corpus:
java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/cikm09/data/www07-classes.txt 5000 4 ../data/cikm09/data/K3/20000.gold_

- Concatenate corpus:
cat 20000.gold_0 20000.gold_1 20000.gold_2 20000.gold_3 > 20000.gold

- Extract feature

Prepare Pantel data

2. Remember: Replacing non-ascii characters before generating features.

3. java -jar Jupiter.jar CreateDataset ../data/acl10/Pantel/pantelConcepts.txt 5000 4 ../data/acl10/Pantel/20000.gold

4. cat 20000.gold0 20000.gold1 20000.gold2 20000.gold3 > 20000.gold

5. java -jar Jupiter.jar PermuteData ../data/acl10/Pantel/20000.gold ../data/acl10/Pantel/20000.shuffled.gold

6. Generate features
